UKR_dualism_category = {
	UKR_hetman_makes_his_move = {
		icon = GFX_decision_shield
		
		allowed = { always = no } #manually activated
		
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = UKR_Prepare_The_Anti_Hetman_Coup
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = "The regime has stabilized"
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = UKR_dnieper_explosion
						has_global_flag = UKR_hetmanate_is_over
						has_global_flag = UKR_konovalets_counet_coup
					}
				}
			}
		}
		available = {
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = UKR_Prepare_The_Anti_Hetman_Coup
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = "The regime has stabilized"
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = UKR_dnieper_explosion
						has_global_flag = UKR_hetmanate_is_over
						has_global_flag = UKR_konovalets_counet_coup
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		is_good = no
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 35
		
		cancel_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision UKR_hetman_makes_his_move"
			UKR_decrease_hetman_strength = yes
			UKR_decrease_hetman = yes
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout UKR_hetman_makes_his_move"
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = UKR_Coalition_With_UVO }
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_1 }
					}
					set_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_1
					country_event = ukrpol.301
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_2 }
					}
					set_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_2
					country_event = ukrpol.17
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_3 }
					}
					set_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_3
					country_event = ukrpol.27
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_4 }
					}
					set_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_4
					country_event = ukrpol.28
				}
				else = {
					UKR_increase_hetman_strength = yes
					UKR_increase_hetman = yes
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = UKR_Coalition_Of_Monarchists }
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_1 }
					}
					set_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_1
					country_event = ukrpol.29
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_2 }
					}
					set_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_2
					country_event = ukrpol.30
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_3 }
					}
					set_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_3
					country_event = ukrpol.19
					hidden_effect = {
						country_event = {
							id = ukrpol.20
							days = 15
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					UKR_increase_hetman_strength = yes
					UKR_increase_hetman = yes
				}
			}
			activate_mission = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move
		}
	}

UKR_pacification = {
	UKR_pacification_generic = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_ignite_civil_war
		allowed = { always = no } # manually activated
		
		available = {
			FROM = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = UKR_rebel_state } }
		}

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = FROM
			}
		}
		visible = { FROM = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = UKR_rebel_state } } }
		custom_cost_text = UKR_CP_pacification
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			check_variable = { command_power > UKR_pacification_cost }
		}
		days_remove = UKR_pacification_decision_time
		fire_only_once = yes
		ai_will_do = { factor = 100 }
		state_target = yes
		on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision complete UKR_pacification_generic target: [From.GetName]"
			add_command_power = -5
		}

		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove UKR_pacification_generic target: [From.GetName]"
			army_experience = 2
			FROM = {
				remove_core_of = UPR
				if = {
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					cancel_resistance = yes
					force_disable_resistance = { clear = yes }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
					}
					remove_claim_by = ROOT
					add_core_of = ROOT
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = UKR_rebel_state }
				if = {
					limit = { is_demilitarized_zone = yes }
					set_demilitarized_zone = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				}
				country_event = ukrpol.37

			}
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout UKR_rivne_uprising"
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
					OR = {
						has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_rivne_uprising option = UKR_RIVNE_UPRISING_DYREKTORIA_DISABLED }
						has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_future option = UKR_FUTURE_HETMAN_DEM  }
						has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_future option = UKR_FUTURE_HETMAN_COSSACK  }
						has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_future option = UKR_FUTURE_HETMAN_AUT  }
						has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_future option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_UMP  }
						has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_future option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_USKHD  }
						has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_future option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_UPSS_SOCIALISM }
						has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_future option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_UPSS_MONSOC }
						has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_future option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_UPSS_CONSERVATIVE }
						has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_future option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_UPSS_CONSERVATIVE_MONARCH }
						has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_future option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_UPSS_BOLBOCHAN }
						has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_future option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_UPSS_BOLBOCHAN_DEMOCRACY }
						has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_future option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_UPSS_HREKIV_JUNTA }
						has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_future option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_UPSS_HREKIV_OTAMANOVSKYI }					
						has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_future option = UKR_FUTURE_UVO_KON  }
					}
				}
				country_event = ukrpol.37
				set_global_flag = UPR_dyrektoria_become_exiled_in_WSU
			}
			else = {
				country_event = ukrpol.36
			}
		}

political_actions = {
	UKR_recruit_teroborona = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_military

		allowed = { original_tag = UKR }
		
		available = {
			has_war_support > 0			
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = UKR_teroborona_is_recruiting
			}
		}
		visible = {
			NOT = { FROM = { has_state_flag = UKR_teroborona_recruited_@ROOT } }
			has_defensive_war = yes
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			has_equipment = { infantry_equipment > 499 }
			command_power > 4
		}
		custom_cost_text = 500_infantry_equipment_1_cp_5
		days_remove = 15
		cancel_if_not_visible = yes
		on_map_mode = map_only

		state_target = yes
		target_array = UKR.owned_states
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_core_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		target_root_trigger = {
			has_idea = UKR_teroborona_idea
			has_defensive_war = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}

		cancel_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision cancel UKR_recruit_teroborona target: [From.GetName]"
			hidden_effect = {
				add_command_power = 5
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = 500
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision UKR_recruit_teroborona target: [From.GetName]"
			set_country_flag = UKR_teroborona_is_recruiting
			hidden_effect = {
				add_command_power = -5
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = -500
				}
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove UKR_recruit_teroborona target: [From.GetName]"
			clr_country_flag = UKR_teroborona_is_recruiting
			FROM = {
				set_state_flag = UKR_teroborona_recruited_@ROOT
				### calculate number of units to spawn
				set_temp_variable = { units_to_spawn = state_population_k }
				divide_temp_variable = { units_to_spawn = 500 }

				### failsafe so at least one unit is always spawned
				clamp_temp_variable = { var = units_to_spawn min = 1 max = 7 }

				### tooltip
				set_temp_variable = { total_units_to_spawn = units_to_spawn }
				custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_recruit_teroborona_units

				### spawn normal militias
				set_temp_variable = { counter = 1 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { var = units_to_spawn value = 1 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
					}
					ROOT = { 
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { has_template = "Teroborona" }
							}
							division_template = {
								name = "Teroborona"
								division_names_group = UKR_MIL_01
								regiments = {
									irregular_infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
									irregular_infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
									irregular_infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
									irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
									irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
								}						
								support = {
									recon = { x = 0 y = 0 }
									military_police = { x = 0 y = 1 }
								}
								priority = 0
								template_counter = 68
							}
						}
					}
					for_loop_effect = {
						start = 1
						end = units_to_spawn
						compare = less_than_or_equals

						meta_effect = {
							text = {
								create_unit = {
									division = "name = [DIVISION] division_template = \"Teroborona\" start_experience_factor = 0.1 start_equipment_factor = 1"
									allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
									owner = ROOT
								}
							}
							DIVISION = "\\\"[?counter]a [THIS.GetName] Okrema Bryhada Teritorialnoi Oborony\\\""
						}
						add_to_temp_variable = { counter = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

		cancel_trigger = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = UKR_crush_the_ukrainian_revolt_tooltip
				any_allied_country = {
					has_capitulated = yes
					capital_scope = {
						var:202.owner = { is_ally_with = var:PREV.controller }
					}
				}
			}
		}

		is_good = no
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 200

		cancel_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision UKR_crush_the_ukrainian_revolt_AUS"
			country_event = ukrfor.304
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout UKR_crush_the_ukrainian_revolt_AUS"
			if = {
				limit = { has_war_with = UKR }
				country_event = ukrfor.304
			}

			}			
		}

			add_to_variable = { UKR_evacuation_cost = 5 }		
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_industry_relocation_complete_effect_tt
			FROM = {

					limit = { arms_factory > 0 }
					set_state_flag = UKR_relocated_arms
					remove_building = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { industrial_complex > 0 }
					set_state_flag = UKR_relocated_ind
					remove_building = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove UKR_evacuate_industry target: [From.GetName]"
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_industry_relocation_remove_effect_tt
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {

						is_west_ukrainian_state = yes

					is_in_home_area = yes

				if = {

							FROM = { arms_factory > 0 }

						}
					}
					FROM = { clr_state_flag = UKR_relocated_arms }

						instant_build = yes
					}

					}

UKR_foreign_policy = {
	UKR_small_pact = {
		icon = GFX_decision_shield
		available = {
			surrender_progress < 0.05
			OR = {
				POL = { has_idea = UKR_EE_cooperation }
				WHR = { has_idea = UKR_EE_cooperation }
			}
			OR = {
				is_in_faction = no
				all_allied_country = {
					OR = {
						is_major = no
						is_subject = yes
						has_capitulated = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_idea = UKR_EE_cooperation
			OR = {
				NOT = { country_exists = GER }
				GER = { has_capitulated = yes }
				is_in_faction = no
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_government = social_democrat
					has_socialist_government = yes
				}
			}
			is_subject = no
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		ai_will_do = { factor = 100 }

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision complete UKR_small_pact"
			add_political_power = 75
			set_country_flag = UKR_small_pact_tree
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = UKR_EE_cooperation
				add_idea = UKR_EE_cooperation2
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_faction_leader = yes } #== took over the Reichspakt
				custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_reichspakt_collapse_warning
				effect_tooltip = { create_faction = small_pact }
				hidden_effect = {
					every_other_country = {
						limit = {
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
							is_subject = no
							OR = {
								has_idea = UKR_EE_cooperation
								UKR_is_potential_small_pact_member = yes
							}
						}
						add_to_temp_array = { small_pact_members_from_reichspakt = THIS }
					}
					leave_faction = yes
					MIE_remove_from_intermarium = yes
					create_faction = small_pact
					for_each_loop = {
						array = small_pact_members_from_reichspakt
						set_global_flag = TEMPORARY_DISABLED_FACTION_POPUP
						add_to_faction = var:v
					}

					### trigger German capitulation and flight to Africa ###
					GER = { country_event = capt.11 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				create_faction = small_pact
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_idea = UKR_EE_cooperation
						UKR_is_potential_small_pact_member = yes
					}
					has_war_with = INT
					OR = {
						is_in_faction = no
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
					OR = {
						is_in_faction = no
						is_subject_of = GER
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				display_individual_scopes = yes
				country_event = ukrfor.650
			}
		}
	}

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout KCN_vote_timer"
			clr_global_flag = KCN_vote_ongoing
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = KCN_cultural_research_cooperation_vote }
				clr_global_flag = KCN_cultural_research_cooperation_vote
				UKR = { country_event = ukrsoc.72 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = KCN_economic_cooperation_vote }
				clr_global_flag = KCN_economic_cooperation_vote
				UKR = { country_event = ukrsoc.69 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = KCN_candidate_membership_vote }
				clr_global_flag = KCN_candidate_membership_vote
				UKR = { country_event = ukrsoc.79 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = KCN_candidate_membership_revoke }
				clr_global_flag = KCN_candidate_membership_revoke
				UKR = { country_event = ukrsoc.87 }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes > global.kcn_no_votes }
					}
					country_event = { id = ukrsoc.68 hours = 2 }
				}
				else = {
					country_event = { id = ukrsoc.67 hours = 2 }
				}
			}
			clear_variable = global.kcn_yes_votes
			clear_variable = global.kcn_no_votes
			clear_variable = global.kcn_abstain_votes
		}
	}
}

							check_variable = { UKR_first_ingridient = 1 }

					}
				}

				custom_effect_tooltip = iron_cowboy_effect	
			}
			else_if = {

						AND = {

	UKR_rise_an_uprising = {
		icon = generic_ignite_civil_war

		available = {
			can_declare_war_on = FROM
		}
		visible = {
			FROM = { owns_state = 91 }
			check_variable = { UKR_galicia_readiness > 1 }
		}

		targets = { 91.OWNER }
		target_root_trigger = { has_country_flag = UKR_preparing_for_galicia_attack }
		target_trigger = {
			can_declare_war_on = FROM
			FROM = { owns_state = 91 }
		}

		cost = 30
		days_remove = 30
		fire_only_once = yes
		war_with_target_on_remove = yes
		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					FROM = { dont_start_major_faction_wars = yes }
					ROOT_is_threatened_cautious = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = { # don't do anything if already at war
				factor = 0
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = { #don't attack if...
				factor = 0
				AUS = {
					is_ally_with = FROM 
					is_faction_leader = yes
					has_war = no
				}
				strength_ratio = { tag = AUS ratio > 2.0 } #ROM isn't stronk
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				AUS = { is_ally_with = FROM } #owner of TRS is AUS or AUS-aligned
				strength_ratio = { tag = AUS ratio > 2.0 }
			}
			modifier = { #attack if uprising starts or ROM is stronk (POL version)
				factor = 20
				POL = {
					is_ally_with = FROM
					NOT = { GER = { is_ally_with = PREV } }
				}
				strength_ratio = { tag = POL ratio > 1.0 }
			}
			modifier = { #don't attack if...
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					AUS = { is_ally_with = FROM }
					GER = { is_ally_with = FROM }
				}
				FROM = { 
					OR = {
						strength_ratio = { tag = ROOT ratio > 1.0 }
						AND = {
							is_in_faction = yes
							faction_leader = {
								is_faction_leader = yes
								surrender_progress < 0.10
								strength_ratio = { tag = ROOT ratio > 1.0 }
							}
						}
						AND = {
							is_subject = yes
							overlord = {
								surrender_progress < 0.10
								strength_ratio = { tag = ROOT ratio > 1.0 }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		cancel_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision cancelled UKR_rise_an_uprising target: [From.GetName]"
			clear_decision_attack_AI = yes
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision UKR_rise_an_uprising target: [From.GetName]"
			setup_decision_attack_AI = yes
			FROM = { country_event = kr.political.30 } #warning event
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { var:91.owner = { tag = GAL } }
					var:91.owner = {
						country_event = {
							id = ukrpol.39
							days = 3
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove UKR_rise_an_uprising target: [From.GetName]"
			clear_decision_attack_AI = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_war_with = var:91.owner }
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = var:91.owner
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = UKR_GAL_revolt
				for_each_scope_loop = {
					array = global.UKR_east_galicia_states
					
					#Remove AUS/HUN/POL armies
					teleport_armies = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								is_ally_with = AUS
								is_ally_with = HUN
								is_ally_with = POL
							}
						}
						to_state_array = owned_controlled_states
					}
					
					#Remove resistance
					if = {
						limit = { has_resistance = yes }
						add_resistance = -100
					}
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = UKR_galician_collaboration }
					if = {
						limit = { 
							ROOT = { UKR_has_socialist_government = yes }
						}
						ROOT = {
							division_template = {
								name = "Halytska Chervona Hvardiia"
								division_names_group = UKR_MIL_01
								regiments = {
									militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
									militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
									militia = { x = 0 y = 2 }
									militia = { x = 1 y = 0 }
									militia = { x = 1 y = 1 }
									militia = { x = 1 y = 2 }
								}
							}
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "division_template = \"Halytska Chervona Hvardiia\" start_experience_factor = 0.1"
							owner = ROOT
							allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
						}
					}
					else = {
						ROOT = {
							division_template = {
								name = "Okrema Halytska Bryhada"
								division_names_group = UKR_MIL_01
								regiments = {
									militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
									militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
									militia = { x = 0 y = 2 }
									militia = { x = 1 y = 0 }
									militia = { x = 1 y = 1 }
									militia = { x = 1 y = 2 }
								}
							}
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "division_template = \"Okrema Halytska Bryhada\" start_experience_factor = 0.1"
							owner = ROOT
							allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_government = national_populist }
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { has_template = "Halytskyi korpus Sichovykh Striltsiv" }
						}
						division_template = {
							name = "Halytskyi korpus Sichovykh Striltsiv"
							division_names_group = UKR_ELI_02
							regiments = {
								elite_infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
								elite_infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
								elite_infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
								elite_infantry = { x = 0 y = 3 }
								elite_infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
								elite_infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
								elite_infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
								infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
								infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
							}
							support = {
								artillery = { x = 0 y = 0 }
								engineer = { x = 0 y = 1 }
								recon = { x = 0 y = 2 }
							}
						}
					}
					random_controlled_state = {
						limit = {
							is_in_array = { global.UKR_east_galicia_states = THIS }
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "division_template = \"Halytskyi korpus Sichovykh Striltsiv\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
							owner = ROOT
						}
					}
					random_controlled_state = {
						limit = {
							is_in_array = { global.UKR_east_galicia_states = THIS }
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "division_template = \"Halytskyi korpus Sichovykh Striltsiv\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"

			UKR_ump_uskhd_in_power = no
		}
		available = {
			has_completed_focus = UKR_Principles_Of_Classocracy
		}
		
		is_good = no
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 86
		
		cancel_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision cancel UKR_change_the_constitution"
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout UKR_change_the_constitution"
			complete_national_focus = UKR_Principles_Of_Classocracy
		}
	}
	UKR_impending_failure_mission = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_factory
		
		allowed = { always = no } #manually activated
		
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = UKR_dont_have_impending_failure
					NOT = {
						has_idea = UKR_impending_failure
						has_idea = UKR_impending_failure_1
						has_idea = UKR_impending_failure_2
						has_idea = UKR_impending_failure_3
						has_idea = UKR_impending_failure_4
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_stability > 0.25
					custom_trigger_tooltip = {
						tooltip = UKR_impending_failure_mission_tt
						check_variable = { party_popularity@ruling_party > 0.5 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}
		
		is_good = no
		fire_only_once = no
		days_mission_timeout = 150
		
		cancel_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision cancel UKR_impending_failure_mission"
			add_stability = 0.1
			add_war_support = 0.1
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_ideas = {
					UKR_impending_failure
					UKR_impending_failure_1
					UKR_impending_failure_2
					UKR_impending_failure_3
					UKR_impending_failure_4
				}
			}
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout UKR_impending_failure_mission"
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = UKR_impending_failure }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = UKR_impending_failure
					add_idea = UKR_impending_failure_1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = UKR_impending_failure_1 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = UKR_impending_failure_1
					add_idea = UKR_impending_failure_2
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = UKR_impending_failure_2 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = UKR_impending_failure_2
					add_idea = UKR_impending_failure_3
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = UKR_impending_failure_3 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = UKR_impending_failure_3
					add_idea = UKR_impending_failure_4
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = UKR_impending_failure_4 }
				add_stability = -0.1
				add_war_support = -0.1
			}
			activate_mission = UKR_impending_failure_mission
		}
	}

						}
					}
				}
			}

					}
				}
				random_list = {
					15 = {
						FROM = {
							add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
						}
					}
					15 = {

MIE_decisions = {
	UKR_seize_leadership_of_mie = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_ignite_civil_war
		allowed = { always = no }
		visible = { NOT = { tag = MIE } }
		
		custom_cost_text = CP_50
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 49.99 }
		
		fire_only_once = yes
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_foreign_policy option = UKR_FOREIGN_POLICY_REICHSPAKT }
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision UKR_seize_leadership_of_mie target: [From.GetName]"
			hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -50 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = "We will become the new leader of EEDC"
			MIE = {
				delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Osteuropäische Interdivision" }
			}
			clear_global_event_target = MIE_leader
			save_global_event_target_as = MIE_leader
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = MIE_armored_division_exists }
				MIE_form_armored_interdivision = yes
			}
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = GER decision = UKR_bye_pakt }
		}
	}
	UKR_bye_pakt = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_ignite_civil_war
		allowed = { always = no }
		available = {
			has_war_with = FRA
			has_capitulated = no
			OR = {
				NOT = { country_exists = GER }
				GER = { surrender_progress > 0.4 }
			}
			GER = {
				has_war_with = FRA
				surrender_progress > 0.4
			}
			
		}
		cost = 0
		
		fire_only_once = yes
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_foreign_policy option = UKR_FOREIGN_POLICY_REICHSPAKT }
			}
			modifier = { #don't risk two-front war
				factor = 0
				has_war_with = var:219.owner 
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision UKR_bye_pakt target: [From.GetName]"
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_owned_by = ROOT
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
					ROOT = { divisions_in_state = { state = PREV size > 0 } }
				}
				teleport_armies = {
					limit = { tag = ROOT }
					to_state_array = owned_controlled_states
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				teleport_armies = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							tag = ROOT
							has_war_with = ROOT
						}
					}
					to_state_array = owned_controlled_states
				}
			}
			remove_puppet_and_leave_faction = yes
			peace_out_non_neighbours_after_leaving_faction = yes
			GER_remove_from_mitteleuropa = yes
			MIE_remove_from_intermarium = yes
			remove_from_all_tech_sharing_groups = yes
			create_faction = "Eastern Europe Defensive Pact"
			every_country = {
				limit = { 
					has_country_flag = MIE_member 
					has_country_flag = MIE_member_will_be_couped
				}
				remove_puppet_and_leave_faction = yes
				peace_out_non_neighbours_after_leaving_faction = yes
				MIE_remove_from_intermarium = yes
				country_event = ukrsun.61
			}
			MIE = { delete_unit = { id = 177013 } }
			clear_global_event_target = MIE_leader
			clr_global_flag = MIE_intermarium_formed
			
		}
	}
	UKR_ally_nationalists_in_country = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_ignite_civil_war
		allowed = { always = no }
		available = {
			FROM = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }	
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {

				tag = MIE

					country_exists = EST
				}
			}
			FROM = { 
				NOT = { has_country_flag = MIE_member_will_be_couped }
			}
		}
		ai_hint_pp_cost = 25
		custom_cost_text = PP_25_CP_25

			has_political_power > 24.99
			command_power > 24.99
		}
		
		fire_only_once = yes
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 100

				has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_foreign_policy option = UKR_FOREIGN_POLICY_REICHSPAKT }
			}

			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove UKR_ally_nationalists_in_country target: [From.GetName]"
			if = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						AND = {
							FROM = {
								tag = POL 
								OR = {
									has_government = authoritarian_democrat
									has_government = national_populist
								}
							}
						}
						AND = {
							FROM = {
								tag = WHR
								has_government = national_populist
							}
						}
					}
				}
				FROM = { country_event = ukrsun.62 }
			}	
			else = {
				effect_tooltip = { country_event = ukrsun.66 }
				hidden_effect = { 
					FROM = { country_event = ukrsun.65 }
				}
			}
